 bajet main jo anya pramukh baaten hai, unamem pramukh steshnon par saat atirikt agjacutive lanj, maanavrahit railway phatakon ko yantrachaalit karne, yatriyon khaskar mahilaon kii suraksha sunishchit karne ke liye railway suraksha bal main vruddhi, railgadiyon kii takkar rokane ke liye nai takaraav rodhi pranali lagu karne, chuninda rail gadiyon main vaai-faai kii suvidha pradaan karne or railgadiyon main gunvattta niyantran ke saath aadhunik rasoigharon kii vyavastha bhi shaamil he
 While presenting the budget, Bansal said in the Lok Sabha, ‚Äúindian Railways is closely associated with the development of the country
 " unhone kaha ki railway ke liye vittiya sthayitv aavashyak he, lekin is baar kiraaya vruddhi nahin hogi, kyonki pichley maah kiraaye kaa punarnirdhaaran kiya ja chukaa he
 However, he proposed to raise some fees for Tatkal and reservation
 shayanyan shrenee main tatkaal tikat ke liye shulk 75 rupee se badhaakar 90 rupee or agjacutive shrenee main 200 rupee se badhaakar 300 rupee karne kaa prastaav kiya gaya he
 In addition, it has been proposed to increase clerk fees between Rs 5 and Rs 10
 saath hi tikat radd karaane kaa shulk 10 se 50 rupee tak badhaayaa gaya he
 5 in freight
 8 pratishat vruddhi kaa prastaav kiya he
 The railway minister expressed happiness that the operating ratio of the railway has come down from 95 paise to 88 paise
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki ek rupee kamaane ke liye bhartiya rail ko ab 88 paise kharch karne padate hai
 The Railway Minister said that railways are the most important source of development of the country
 yah ek mahatvapurn sanghathan he, jo desh ko uttar main jammu evam kashmir ke baraamula se dakshin main kanyakumari or pashchim main dwarka se purab main ledo ko jodta he
 The country's railway network spans 64,000 kilometers, with 7,083 stations
 kareeb 12,000 yatri railgadiyaan pratidin 2
 3 crore passengers to their destinations, while 7,000 freight trains 26
 5 lakh ton vastuon kii dhulaai karti hai
 It employs about 14 lakh people
 bansal ne yah bhi kaha ki vah iarsitisi kii website se aarakshan karaane waalon kii mushkilon se waakif hai or isliye nai i-tikating pranali shuru kii jaaegi, jisase online tikat booking kii gati tej hogi
 He said that the new system will have the capacity to book 7,200 tickets within a minute, while the current capacity is to book 2,000 tickets in a minute
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne jahaan bajet ko sudharatmak or pragatisheel bataaya he, vahiin vipaksh ne isaki aalochana kii he
 Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) President Rajnath Singh said that this railway budget reflected the inefficiency and lack of vision of the United Progressive Alliance (UPA) government
 tippaniyan Businessmen of the country described the railway budget as soft and balanced in the current economic situation
 bhartiya udyog parisangh ke mahanideshak chandrajit banerjee ne kaha, "vittiya vyavhaaryata or anushaasan par jod diya janaa swaagat yogya kadam he
 Financial discipline, security and passenger comfort are essential to the health of this transport vehicle, which the common people use
 mantri ne in par samuchit dhyaan diya he
 " associated chambers of commers and industry (asocham) ne rail bajet ko naram bataaya or kaha ki sarkaar prabhavi corporatikaran ke avasar kaa laabh uthaane se chook gai
 Rajkumar Dhoot, President of Assocham, said, ‚Äúthe limit of railway capacity should be dealt with first
 
 This could have been noticed in the railway budget
 " The good news for those making reservations with IRCTC is that it has been proposed to introduce a new e-ticketing system in view of the increasing burden on this website and the problems faced by people due to its slow pace
 rail bajet main kareeb 106 nai railgadiyaan chalaane kaa prastaav kiya gaya he

 chuninda railgadiyon main adhik suvidha sampann coach lagane or pramukh steshnon par swachaalit seedhiyaan lagane kaa bhi prastaav he
 63,363 crore (633) by Railway Minister Bansal
 63 arab rupee yaa 11
 5 billion dollar) railway budget
 yah unka pehla bajet he
 He is the first Congress Minister to present the Railway Budget in the last 17 years
 varsh 2014 main prastaavit aam chunaav ko dekhte hue bajet ko 'loklubhaavan' banane kaa prayaas kiya gaya he
 Other key things in the budget include seven additional executive lounges at major stations, mechanized unmanned railway gates, increased railway security force to ensure safety of passengers, especially women, new anti-collision system implemented to prevent train collisions To provide wi-fi facilities in selected trains and quality control in trains Also included is the arrangement of modern kitchens
 bansal ne bajet pesh karte hue loksabhaa main kaha, "bhartiya railway desh ke vikaas se ghanishtha rup se sambhddha he
 "he said that financial stability is necessary for the railways, but this time the fare will not increase, as the fare has been rescheduled last month
 unhone haalanki tatkaal tathaa aarakshan ke liye kuch shulk badhaane kaa prastaav kiya
 It has been proposed to increase the fee from Rs 75 to Rs 90 for Tatkal tickets in Sleeper class and Rs 200 to Rs 300 in Executive category
 iske atirikt clerk shulk bhi paanch se 10 rupee ke bich badhaane kaa prastaav kiya gaya he
 Also, the ticket cancellation fee has been increased from 10 to 50 rupees
 maal bhaade main 5
 8 percent increase is proposed
 railmantri ne is baat par khushi jataai ki railway kaa sanchaalan anupaat 95 paise se ghatakar 88 paise par aa gaya he
 This means that Indian Railways now have to spend 88 paise to earn one rupee
 railmantri ne kaha ki railway desh ke vikaas kaa sarvaadhik mahatvapurn strot he
 It is an important organization that connects the country with Baramulla in Jammu and Kashmir in the north, Kanyakumari in the south and Dwarka in the west to Ledo in the east
 desh kaa railway network 64,000 kilometre tak failaa he, jisamen 7,083 stesan hai
 Around 12,000 passenger trains 2 per day
 3 karod yatriyon ko unke gantavy tak pahunchaati hai, jabaki 7,000 malgadiyaan 26
 Carries 5 lakh tons of goods
 isamen kareeb 14 lakh log karyrat hai
 Bansal also said that he is aware of the difficulties faced by those making reservations through the IRCTC website and hence a new e-ticketing system will be introduced, which will speed up the online ticket booking
 unhone kaha ki nai pranali main ek minute ke bheetar 7,200 tikat book karne kii kshamta hogi, jabaki maujuuda kshamta ek minute main 2,000 tikat book karne kii he
 While Prime Minister Manmohan Singh has described the budget as corrective and progressive, the opposition has criticized it
 bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) ke adhyaksh rajnath singh ne kaha ki is rail bajet se sanyukt pragatisheel gathbandhan (samprag) sarkaar kii aakshamata or drushti kaa abhaav parilakshith hota he
 The comments rail bajet ko desh ke kaarobaariyon ne maujuuda aarthik sthiti main naram or santulit bataaya
 Chandrajeet Banerjee, director general of Confederation of Indian Industry, said, "adding on financial viability and discipline is a welcome step
 vittiya anushaasan, suraksha or yatri suvidha is parivahan saadhan ke swasthya ke liye aavashyak he, jiskaa aam log istemaal karte hai
 The minister has given proper attention to these
 " The Associated Chambers of Commerce and Industry (assocham) termed the railway budget as soft and said the government missed out on the opportunity of effective corporatization
 asocham ke adhyaksh rajkumaar dhoot ne kaha, "railway kii kshamta kii seemaa se sabase pehle nipta janaa chahie

 What is Citizenship Amendment Bill? Citizenship Amendment Bill is for Hindus, Sikhs, Buddhists, Jains, Parsis and Christians who have come to India from Pakistan, Afghanistan, Bangladesh without valid travel documents, or whose legal documents have expired in recent years , Enabling them to achieve Indian citizenship
